line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo(); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 42</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 5, 6 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 11</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 0, 42 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 42</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 5 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 36</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 5, undefined ); &nbsp; &nbsp;// 36 &lt;-- `undefined` is missing</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 5, null ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 5 &nbsp;&lt;-- null coerces to `0`</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( undefined, 6 ); &nbsp; &nbsp;// 17 &lt;-- `undefined` is missing</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( null, 6 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 6 &nbsp;&lt;-- null coerces to `0`</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Notice the results and how they imply both subtle differences and similarities to the earlier approaches.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">x = 11 in a function declaration is more like x !== undefined ? x : 11 than the much more common idiom x || 11, so you'll need to be careful in converting your pre-ES6 code to this ES6 default parameter value syntax.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: A rest/gather parameter (see "Spread/Rest") cannot have a default value. So, while function foo(...vals=[1,2,3]) { might seem an intriguing capability, it's not valid syntax. You'll need to continue to apply that sort of logic manually if necessary.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Default Value Expressions</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Function default values can be more than just simple values like 31; they can be any valid expression, even a function call:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function bar(val) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( "bar called!" );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; return y + val;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function foo(x = y + 3, z = bar( x )) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( x, z );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var y = 5;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo(); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// "bar called"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 8 13</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( 10 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// "bar called"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 10 15</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">y = 6;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo( undefined, 10 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 9 10</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">As you can see, the default value expressions are lazily evaluated, meaning they're only run if and when they're needed -- that is, when a parameter's argument is omitted or is undefined.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">It's a subtle detail, but the formal parameters in a function declaration are in their own scope (think of it as a scope bubble wrapped around just the ( .. ) of the function declaration), not in the function body's scope. That means a reference to an identifier in a default value expression first matches the formal parameters' scope before looking to an outer scope. See the Scope &amp; Closures title of this series for more information.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var w = 1, z = 2;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function foo( x = w + 1, y = x + 1, z = z + 1 ) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( x, y, z );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo(); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// ReferenceError</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The w in the w + 1 default value expression looks for w in the formal parameters' scope, but does not find it, so the outer scope's w is used. Next, The x in the x + 1 default value expression finds x in the formal parameters' scope, and luckily x has already been initialized, so the assignment to y works fine.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">However, the z in z + 1 finds z as a not-yet-initialized-at-that-moment parameter variable, so it never tries to find the z from the outer scope.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">As we mentioned in the "let Declarations" section earlier in this chapter, ES6 has a TDZ, which prevents a variable from being accessed in its uninitialized state. As such, the z + 1 default value expression throws a TDZReferenceError error.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Though it's not necessarily a good idea for code clarity, a default value expression can even be an inline function expression call -- commonly referred to as an immediately invoked function expression (IIFE):</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function foo( x =</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; (function(v){ return v + 11; })( 31 )</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( x );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">foo(); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 42</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">There will very rarely be any cases where an IIFE (or any other executed inline function expression) will be appropriate for default value expressions. If you find yourself tempted to do this, take a step back and reevaluate!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: If the IIFE had tried to access the x identifier and had not declared its own x, this would also have been a TDZ error, just as discussed before.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The default value expression in the previous snippet is an IIFE in that in the sense that it's a function that's executed right inline, via (31). If we had left that part off, the default value assigned to x would have just been a function reference itself, perhaps like a default callback. There will probably be cases where that pattern will be quite useful, such as:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function ajax(url, cb = function(){}) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">ajax( "http://some.url.1" );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In this case, we essentially want to default cb to be a no-op empty function call if not otherwise specified. The function expression is just a function reference, not a function call itself (no invoking () on the end of it), which accomplishes that goal.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Since the early days of JS, there's been a little-known but useful quirk available to us: Function.prototype is itself an empty no-op function. So, the declaration could have been cb = Function.prototype and saved the inline function expression creation.</span></font></h2>
### Destructuring
<h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Destructuring</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">ES6 introduces a new syntactic feature called destructuring, which may be a little less confusing if you instead think of it as structured assignment. To understand this meaning, consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function foo() {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; return [1,2,3];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var tmp = foo(),</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a = tmp[0], b = tmp[1], c = tmp[2];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">As you can see, we created a manual assignment of the values in the array that foo() returns to individual variables a,b, and c, and to do so we (unfortunately) needed the tmp variable.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Similarly, we can do the following with objects:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function bar() {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; return {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; x: 4,</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; y: 5,</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z: 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var tmp = bar(),</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; x = tmp.x, y = tmp.y, z = tmp.z;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The tmp.x property value is assigned to the x variable, and likewise for tmp.y to y and tmp.z to z.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Manually assigning indexed values from an array or properties from an object can be thought of as structured assignment. ES6 adds a dedicated syntax for destructuring, specifically array destructuring and object destructuring. This syntax eliminates the need for the tmp variable in the previous snippets, making them much cleaner. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var [ a, b, c ] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x: x, y: y, z: z } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You're likely more accustomed to seeing syntax like [a,b,c] on the righthand side of an = assignment, as the value being assigned.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Destructuring symmetrically flips that pattern, so that [a,b,c] on the lefthand side of the = assignment is treated as a kind of "pattern" for decomposing the righthand side array value into separate variable assignments.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Similarly, { x: x, y: y, z: z } specifies a "pattern" to decompose the object value from bar() into separate variable assignments.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Object Property Assignment Pattern</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Let's dig into that { x: x, .. } syntax from the previous snippet. If the property name being matched is the same as the variable you want to declare, you can actually shorten the syntax:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x, y, z } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Pretty cool, right?</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">But is { x, .. } leaving off the x: part or leaving off the : x part? We're actually leaving off the x: part when we use the shorter syntax. That may not seem like an important detail, but you'll understand its importance in just a moment.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If you can write the shorter form, why would you ever write out the longer form? Because that longer form actually allows you to assign a property to a different variable name, which can sometimes be quite useful:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x: bam, y: baz, z: bap } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( bam, baz, bap ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ReferenceError</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">There's a subtle but super-important quirk to understand about this variation of the object destructuring form. To illustrate why it can be a gotcha you need to be careful of, let's consider the "pattern" of how normal object literals are specified:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var X = 10, Y = 20;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = { a: X, b: Y };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o.a, o.b ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 10 20</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In { a: X, b: Y }, we know that a is the object property, and X is the source value that gets assigned to it. In other words, the syntactic pattern is target: source, or more obviously, property-alias: value. We intuitively understand this because it's the same as = assignment, where the pattern is target = source.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">However, when you use object destructuring assignment -- that is, putting the { .. } object literal-looking syntax on the lefthand side of the = operator -- you invert that target: source pattern.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Recall:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x: bam, y: baz, z: bap } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The syntactic pattern here is source: target (or value: variable-alias). x: bam means the x property is the source value and bam is the target variable to assign to. In other words, object literals are target &lt;-- source, and object destructuring assignments are source --&gt; target. See how that's flipped?</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">There's another way to think about this syntax though, which may help ease the confusion. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var aa = 10, bb = 20;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = { x: aa, y: bb };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var &nbsp; &nbsp; { x: AA, y: BB } = o;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( AA, BB ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 10 20</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In the { x: aa, y: bb } line, the x and y represent the object properties. In the { x: AA, y: BB } line, the x and they also represent the object properties.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Recall how earlier I asserted that { x, .. } was leaving off the x: part? In those two lines, if you erase the x: andy: parts in that snippet, you're left only with aa, bb and AA, BB, which in effect -- only conceptually, not actually -- are assignments from aa to AA and from bb to BB.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">So, that symmetry may help to explain why the syntactic pattern was intentionally flipped for this ES6 feature.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: I would have preferred the syntax to be { AA: x , BB: y } for the destructuring assignment, as that would have preserved consistency of the more familiar target: source pattern for both usages. Alas, I'm having to train my brain for the inversion, as some readers may also have to do.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Not Just Declarations</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">So far, we've used destructuring assignment with var declarations (of course, they could also use let and const), but destructuring is a general assignment operation, not just a declaration.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a, b, c, x, y, z;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[a,b,c] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { x, y, z } = bar() );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The variables can already be declared, and then the destructuring only does assignments, exactly as we've already seen.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: For the object destructuring form specifically, when leaving off a var/let/const declarator, we had to surround the whole assignment expression in ( ), because otherwise the { .. } on the lefthand side as the first element in the statement is taken to be a block statement instead of an object.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;
