margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In fact, the assignment expressions (a, y, etc.) don't actually need to be just variable identifiers. Anything that's a valid assignment expression is allowed. For example:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[o.a, o.b, o.c] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { x: o.x, y: o.y, z: o.z } = bar() );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o.a, o.b, o.c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o.x, o.y, o.z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You can even use computed property expressions in the destructuring. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var which = "x",</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; o = {};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { [which]: o[which] } = bar() );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o.x ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The [which]: part is the computed property, which results in x -- the property to destructure from the object in question as the source of the assignment. The o[which] part is just a normal object key reference, which equates too.x as the target of the assignment.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You can use the general assignments to create object mappings/transformations, such as:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; o2 = {};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { a: o2.x, b: o2.y, c: o2.z } = o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o2.x, o2.y, o2.z ); &nbsp; &nbsp;// 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Or you can map an object to an array, such as:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a2 = [];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { a: a2[0], b: a2[1], c: a2[2] } = o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a2 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// [1,2,3]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Or the other way around:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a1 = [ 1, 2, 3 ],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; o2 = {};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[ o2.a, o2.b, o2.c ] = a1;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( o2.a, o2.b, o2.c ); &nbsp; &nbsp;// 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Or you could reorder one array to another:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a1 = [ 1, 2, 3 ],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a2 = [];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[ a2[2], a2[0], a2[1] ] = a1;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a2 ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// [2,3,1]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You can even solve the traditional "swap two variables" task without a temporary variable:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var x = 10, y = 20;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[ y, x ] = [ x, y ];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 20 10</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: Be careful: you shouldn't mix in declaration with assignment unless you want all of the assignment expressions also to be treated as declarations. Otherwise, you'll get syntax errors. That's why in the earlier example I had to do var a2 = [] separately from the [ a2[0], .. ] = .. destructuring assignment. It wouldn't make any sense to try var [ a2[0], .. ] = .., because a2[0] isn't a valid declaration identifier; it also obviously couldn't implicitly create a var a2 = [] declaration to use.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Repeated Assignments</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The object destructuring form allows a source property (holding any value type) to be listed multiple times. For example:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { a: X, a: Y } = { a: 1 };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">X; &nbsp;// 1</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Y; &nbsp;// 1</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">That also means you can both destructure a sub-object/array property and also capture the sub-object/array's value itself. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { a: { x: X, x: Y }, a } = { a: { x: 1 } };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">X; &nbsp;// 1</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Y; &nbsp;// 1</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">a; &nbsp;// { x: 1 }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { a: X, a: Y, a: [ Z ] } = { a: [ 1 ] } );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">X.push( 2 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Y[0] = 10;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">X; &nbsp;// [10,2]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Y; &nbsp;// [10,2]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Z; &nbsp;// 1</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">A word of caution about destructuring: it may be tempting to list destructuring assignments all on a single line as has been done thus far in our discussion. However, it's a much better idea to spread destructuring assignment patterns over multiple lines, using proper indentation -- much like you would in JSON or with an object literal value -- for readability sake.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// harder to read:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { a: { b: [ c, d ], e: { f } }, g } = obj;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// better:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a: {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; b: [ c, d ],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; e: { f }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; g</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">} = obj;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Remember: the purpose of destructuring is not just less typing, but more declarative readability.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Destructuring Assignment Expressions</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The assignment expression with object or array destructuring has as its completion value the full righthand object/array value. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = { a:1, b:2, c:3 },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a, b, c, p;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">p = { a, b, c } = o;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">p === o; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// true</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In the previous snippet, p was assigned the o object reference, not one of the a, b, or c values. The same is true of array destructuring:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = [1,2,3],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a, b, c, p;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">p = [ a, b, c ] = o;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">p === o; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// true</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">By carrying the object/array value through as the completion, you can chain destructuring assignment expressions together:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = { a:1, b:2, c:3 },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; p = [4,5,6],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; a, b, c, x, y, z;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( {a} = {b,c} = o );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">[x,y] = [z] = p;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 4</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Too Many, Too Few, Just Enough</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">With both array destructuring assignment and object destructuring assignment, you do not have to assign all the values that are present. For example:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var [,b] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x, z } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( b, x, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 2 4 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The 1 and 3 values that came back from foo() are discarded, as is the 5 value from bar().</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Similarly, if you try to assign more values than are present in the value you're destructuring/decomposing, you get graceful fallback to undefined, as you'd expect:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var [,,c,d] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { w, z } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( c, z ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 3 6</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( d, w ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// undefined undefined</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">This behavior follows symmetrically from the earlier stated "undefined is missing" principle.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">We examined the ... operator earlier in this chapter, and saw that it can sometimes be used to spread an array value out into its separate values, and sometimes it can be used to do the opposite: to gather a set of values together into an array.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In addition to the gather/rest usage in function declarations, ... can perform the same behavior in destructuring assignments. To illustrate, let's recall a snippet from earlier in this chapter:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a = [2,3,4];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var b = [ 1, ...a, 5 ];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( b ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // [1,2,3,4,5]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Here we see that ...a is spreading a out, because it appears in the array [ .. ] value position. If ...a appears in an array destructuring position, it performs the gather behavior:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a = [2,3,4];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var [ b, ...c ] = a;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( b, c ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 2 [3,4]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The var [ .. ] = a destructuring assignment spreads a out to be assigned to the pattern described inside the [ .. ]. The first part names b for the first value in a (2). But then ...c gathers the rest of the values (3 and 4) into an array and calls it c.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: We've seen how ... works with arrays, but what about with objects? It's not an ES6 feature, but see Chapter 8 for discussion of a possible "beyond ES6" feature where ... works with spreading or gathering objects.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Default Value Assignment</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Both forms of destructuring can offer a default value option for an assignment, using the = syntax similar to the default function argument values discussed earlier.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var [ a = 3, b = 6, c = 9, d = 12 ] = foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x = 5, y = 10, z = 15, w = 20 } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a, b, c, d ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 1 2 3 12</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z, w ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// 4 5 6 20</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You can combine the default value assignment with the alternative assignment expression syntax covered earlier. For example:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var { x, y, z, w: WW = 20 } = bar();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x, y, z, WW ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 4 5 6 20</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Be careful about confusing yourself (or other developers who read your code) if you use an object or array as the default value in a destructuring. You can create some really hard to understand code:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var x = 200, y = 300, z = 100;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = { x: { y: 42 }, z: { y: z } };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { y: x = { y: y } } = o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { z: y = { y: z } } = o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">( { x: z = { y: x } } = o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Can you tell from that snippet what values x, y, and z have at the end? Takes a moment of pondering, I would imagine. I'll end the suspense:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( x.y, y.y, z.y ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 300 100 42</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative;
