We'll cover them in "Arrow Functions" later in this chapter.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The partially redeeming news is that our something(x,y) concise method won't be totally anonymous. See "Function Names" in Chapter 7 for information about ES6 function name inference rules. That won't help us for our recursion, but it helps with debugging at least.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">So what are we left to conclude about concise methods? They're short and sweet, and a nice convenience. But you should only use them if you're never going to need them to do recursion or event binding/unbinding. Otherwise, stick to your old-school something: function something(..) method definitions.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">A lot of your methods are probably going to benefit from concise method definitions, so that's great news! Just be careful of the few where there's an un-naming hazard.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">ES5 Getter/Setter</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Technically, ES5 defined getter/setter literals forms, but they didn't seem to get used much, mostly due to the lack of transpilers to handle that new syntax (the only major new syntax added in ES5, really). So while it's not a new ES6 feature, we'll briefly refresh on that form, as it's probably going to be much more useful with ES6 going forward.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; __id: 10,</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; get id() { return this.__id++; },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; set id(v) { this.__id = v; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.id; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 10</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.id; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 11</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.id = 20;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.id; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 20</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// and:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.__id; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 21</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o.__id; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // 21 -- still!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">These getter and setter literal forms are also present in classes; see Chapter 3.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: It may not be obvious, but the setter literal must have exactly one declared parameter; omitting it or listing others is illegal syntax. The single required parameter can use destructuring and defaults (e.g., set id({ id: v = 0 }) { .. }), but the gather/rest ... is not allowed (set id(...v) { .. }).</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Computed Property Names</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You've probably been in a situation like the following snippet, where you have one or more property names that come from some sort of expression and thus can't be put into the object literal:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var prefix = "user_";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; baz: function(..){ .. }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o[ prefix + "foo" ] = function(..){ .. };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o[ prefix + "bar" ] = function(..){ .. };</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">ES6 adds a syntax to the object literal definition which allows you to specify an expression that should be computed, whose result is the property name assigned. Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var prefix = "user_";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; baz: function(..){ .. },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; [ prefix + "foo" ]: function(..){ .. },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; [ prefix + "bar" ]: function(..){ .. }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Any valid expression can appear inside the [ .. ] that sits in the property name position of the object literal definition.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Probably the most common use of computed property names will be with Symbols (which we cover in "Symbols" later in this chapter), such as:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; [Symbol.toStringTag]: "really cool thing",</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Symbol.toStringTag is a special built-in value, which we evaluate with the [ .. ] syntax, so we can assign the "really cool thing" value to the special property name.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Computed property names can also appear as the name of a concise method or a concise generator:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; ["f" + "oo"]() { .. } &nbsp; // computed concise method</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; *["b" + "ar"]() { .. } &nbsp;// computed concise generator</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Setting [[Prototype]]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">We won't cover prototypes in detail here, so for more information, see the this &amp; Object Prototypes title of this series.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Sometimes it will be helpful to assign the [[Prototype]] of an object at the same time you're declaring its object literal. The following has been a nonstandard extension in many JS engines for a while, but is standardized as of ES6:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o2 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; __proto__: o1,</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o2 is declared with a normal object literal, but it's also [[Prototype]]-linked to o1. The __proto__ property name here can also be a string "__proto__", but note that it cannot be the result of a computed property name (see the previous section).</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">__proto__ is controversial, to say the least. It's a decades-old proprietary extension to JS that is finally standardized, somewhat begrudgingly it seems, in ES6. Many developers feel it shouldn't ever be used. In fact, it's in "Annex B" of ES6, which is the section that lists things JS feels it has to standardize for compatibility reasons only.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: Though I'm narrowly endorsing __proto__ as a key in an object literal definition, I definitely do not endorse using it in its object property form, like o.__proto__. That form is both a getter and setter (again for compatibility reasons), but there are definitely better options. See the this &amp; Object Prototypes title of this series for more information.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">For setting the [[Prototype]] of an existing object, you can use the ES6 utility Object.setPrototypeOf(..). Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o2 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Object.setPrototypeOf( o2, o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: We'll discuss Object again in Chapter 6. "Object.setPrototypeOf(..) Static Function" provides additional details on Object.setPrototypeOf(..). Also see "Object.assign(..) Static Function" for another form that relates o2prototypically to o1.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Object super</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">super is typically thought of as being only related to classes. However, due to JS's classless-objects-with-prototypes nature, super is equally effective, and nearly the same in behavior, with plain objects' concise methods.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o1 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; foo() {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( "o1:foo" );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o2 = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; foo() {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; super.foo();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( "o2:foo" );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Object.setPrototypeOf( o2, o1 );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">o2.foo(); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // o1:foo</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // o2:foo</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: super is only allowed in concise methods, not regular function expression properties. It also is only allowed in super.XXX form (for property/method access), not in super() form.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The super reference in the o2.foo() method is locked statically to o2, and specifically to the [[Prototype]] of o2.super here would basically be Object.getPrototypeOf(o2) -- resolves to o1 of course -- which is how it finds and callso1.foo().</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">For complete details on super, see "Classes" in Chapter 3.</span></font></h2>
### Template Literals
<h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Template Literals</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">At the very outset of this section, I'm going to have to call out the name of this ES6 feature as being awfully... misleading, depending on your experiences with what the word template means.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Many developers think of templates as being reusable renderable pieces of text, such as the capability provided by most template engines (Mustache, Handlebars, etc.). ES6's use of the word template would imply something similar, like a way to declare inline template literals that can be re-rendered. However, that's not at all the right way to think about this feature.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">So, before we go on, I'm renaming to what it should have been called: interpolated string literals (or interpoliterals for short).</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">You're already well aware of declaring string literals with " or ' delimiters, and you also know that these are not smart strings (as some languages have), where the contents would be parsed for interpolation expressions.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">However, ES6 introduces a new type of string literal, using the ` backtick as the delimiter. These string literals allow basic string interpolation expressions to be embedded, which are then automatically parsed and evaluated.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Here's the old pre-ES6 way:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var name = "Kyle";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var greeting = "Hello " + name + "!";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( greeting ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// "Hello Kyle!"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( typeof greeting ); &nbsp; &nbsp; // "string"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Now, consider the new ES6 way:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var name = "Kyle";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var greeting = `Hello ${name}!`;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( greeting ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// "Hello Kyle!"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( typeof greeting ); &nbsp; &nbsp; // "string"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">As you can see, we used the `..` around a series of characters, which are interpreted as a string literal, but any expressions of the form ${..} are parsed and evaluated inline immediately. The fancy term for such parsing and evaluating is interpolation (much more accurate than templating).</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The result of the interpolated string literal expression is just a plain old normal string, assigned to the greeting variable.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: typeof greeting == "string" illustrates why it's important not to think of these entities as special template values, as you cannot assign the unevaluated form of the literal to something and reuse it. The `..` string literal is more like an IIFE in the sense that it's automatically evaluated inline. The result of a `..` string literal is, simply, just a string.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">One really nice benefit of interpolated string literals is they are allowed to split across multiple lines:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var text =</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">`Now is the time for all good men</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">to come to the aid of their</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">country!`;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( text );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// Now is the time for all good men</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// to come to the aid of their</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// country!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The line breaks (newlines) in the interpolated string literal were preserved in the string value.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Unless appearing as explicit escape sequences in the literal value, the value of the \r carriage return character (code point U+000D) or the value of the \r\n carriage return + line feed sequence (code points U+000D and U+000A) are both normalized to a \n line feed character (code point U+000A). Don't worry though; this normalization is rare and would likely only happen if copy-pasting text into your JS file.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Interpolated Expressions</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Any valid expression is allowed to appear inside ${..} in an interpolated string literal, including function calls, inline function expression calls, and even other interpolated string literals!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">function upper(s) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; return s.toUpperCase();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var who = "reader";</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;
