line-height: 30.0125px;">console.log( a ); &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // [2,4,6,8,10]</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In those cases, where you have such inline function expressions, and they fit the pattern of computing a quick calculation in a single statement and returning that result, arrow functions indeed look to be an attractive and lightweight alternative to the more verbose function keyword and syntax.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Most people tend to ooh and aah at nice terse examples like that, as I imagine you just did!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">However, I would caution you that it would seem to me somewhat a misapplication of this feature to use arrow function syntax with otherwise normal, multistatement functions, especially those that would otherwise be naturally expressed as function declarations.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Recall the dollabillsyall(..) string literal tag function from earlier in this chapter -- let's change it to use =&gt; syntax:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var dollabillsyall = (strings, ...values) =&gt;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; strings.reduce( (s,v,idx) =&gt; {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (idx &gt; 0) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (typeof values[idx-1] == "number") {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // look, also using interpolated</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // string literals!</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s += `$${values[idx-1].toFixed( 2 )}`;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s += values[idx-1];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return s + v;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }, "" );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In this example, the only modifications I made were the removal of function, return, and some { .. }, and then the insertion of =&gt; and a var. Is this a significant improvement in the readability of the code? Meh.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">I'd actually argue that the lack of return and outer { .. } partially obscures the fact that the reduce(..) call is the only statement in the dollabillsyall(..) function and that its result is the intended result of the call. Also, the trained eye that is so used to hunting for the word function in code to find scope boundaries now needs to look for the =&gt;marker, which can definitely be harder to find in the thick of the code.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">While not a hard-and-fast rule, I'd say that the readability gains from =&gt; arrow function conversion are inversely proportional to the length of the function being converted. The longer the function, the less =&gt; helps; the shorter the function, the more =&gt; can shine.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">I think it's probably more sensible and reasonable to adopt =&gt; for the places in code where you do need short inline function expressions, but leave your normal-length main functions as is.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Not Just Shorter Syntax, But this</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Most of the popular attention toward =&gt; has been on saving those precious keystrokes by dropping function,return, and { .. } from your code.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">But there's a big detail we've skipped over so far. I said at the beginning of the section that =&gt; functions are closely related to this binding behavior. In fact, =&gt; arrow functions are primarily designed to alter this behavior in a specific way, solving a particular and common pain point with this-aware coding.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The saving of keystrokes is a red herring, a misleading sideshow at best.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Let's revisit another example from earlier in this chapter:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var controller = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; makeRequest: function(..){</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; var self = this;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; btn.addEventListener( "click", function(){</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.makeRequest(..);</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }, false );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">We used the var self = this hack, and then referenced self.makeRequest(..), because inside the callback function we're passing to addEventListener(..), the this binding will not be the same as it is in makeRequest(..) itself. In other words, because this bindings are dynamic, we fall back to the predictability of lexical scope via the self variable.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Herein we finally can see the primary design characteristic of =&gt; arrow functions. Inside arrow functions, the thisbinding is not dynamic, but is instead lexical. In the previous snippet, if we used an arrow function for the callback,this will be predictably what we wanted it to be.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var controller = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; makeRequest: function(..){</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; btn.addEventListener( "click", () =&gt; {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; this.makeRequest(..);</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }, false );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Lexical this in the arrow function callback in the previous snippet now points to the same value as in the enclosingmakeRequest(..) function. In other words, =&gt; is a syntactic stand-in for var self = this.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In cases where var self = this (or, alternatively, a function .bind(this) call) would normally be helpful, =&gt; arrow functions are a nicer alternative operating on the same prinicple. Sounds great, right?</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Not quite so simple.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If =&gt; replaces var self = this or .bind(this) and it helps, guess what happens if you use =&gt; with a this-aware function that doesn't need var self = this to work? You might be able to guess that it's going to mess things up. Yeah.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Consider:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var controller = {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; makeRequest: (..) =&gt; {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; this.helper(..);</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; },</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; helper: (..) =&gt; {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ..</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">controller.makeRequest(..);</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Although we invoke as controller.makeRequest(..), the this.helper reference fails, because this here doesn't point to controller as it normally would. Where does it point? It lexically inherits this from the surrounding scope. In this previous snippet, that's the global scope, where this points to the global object. Ugh.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In addition to lexical this, arrow functions also have lexical arguments -- they don't have their own arguments array but instead inherit from their parent -- as well as lexical super and new.target (see "Classes" in Chapter 3).</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">So now we can conclude a more nuanced set of rules for when =&gt; is appropriate and not:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If you have a short, single-statement inline function expression, where the only statement is a return of some computed value, and that function doesn't already make a this reference inside it, and there's no self-reference (recursion, event binding/unbinding), and you don't reasonably expect the function to ever be that way, you can probably safely refactor it to be an =&gt; arrow function.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If you have an inner function expression that's relying on a var self = this hack or a .bind(this) call on it in the enclosing function to ensure proper this binding, that inner function expression can probably safely become an=&gt; arrow function.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If you have an inner function expression that's relying on something like var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments) in the enclosing function to make a lexical copy of arguments, that inner function expression can probably safely become an =&gt; arrow function.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">For everything else -- normal function declarations, longer multistatment function expressions, functions that need a lexical name identifier self-reference (recursion, etc.), and any other function that doesn't fit the previous characteristics -- you should probably avoid =&gt; function syntax.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Bottom line: =&gt; is about lexical binding of this, arguments, and super. These are intentional features designed to fix some common problems, not bugs, quirks, or mistakes in ES6.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Don't believe any hype that =&gt; is primarily, or even mostly, about fewer keystrokes. Whether you save keystrokes or waste them, you should know exactly what you are intentionally doing with every character typed.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Tip: If you have a function that for any of these articulated reasons is not a good match for an =&gt; arrow function, but it's being declared as part of an object literal, recall from "Concise Methods" earlier in this chapter that there's another option for shorter function syntax.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">If you prefer a visual decision chart for how/why to pick an arrow function:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for..of Loops</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Joining the for and for..in loops from the JavaScript we're all familiar with, ES6 adds a for..of loop, which loops over the set of values produced by an iterator.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The value you loop over with for..of must be an iterable, or it must be a value which can be coerced/boxed to an object (see the Types &amp; Grammar title of this series) that is an iterable. An iterable is simply an object that is able to produce an iterator, which the loop then uses.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Let's compare for..of to for..in to illustrate the difference:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a = ["a","b","c","d","e"];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (var idx in a) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( idx );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// 0 1 2 3 4</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (var val of a) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( val );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// "a" "b" "c" "d" "e"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">As you can see, for..in loops over the keys/indexes in the a array, while for..of loops over the values in a.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Here's the pre-ES6 version of the for..of from that previous snippet:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a = ["a","b","c","d","e"],</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; k = Object.keys( a );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (var val, i = 0; i &lt; k.length; i++) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; val = a[ k[i] ];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( val );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// "a" "b" "c" "d" "e"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">And here's the ES6 but non-for..of equivalent, which also gives a glimpse at manually iterating an iterator (see "Iterators" in Chapter 3):</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var a = ["a","b","c","d","e"];</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (var val, ret, it = a[Symbol.iterator]();</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; (ret = it.next()) &amp;&amp; !ret.done;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; val = ret.value;</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( val );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// "a" "b" "c" "d" "e"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Under the covers, the for..of loop asks the iterable for an iterator (using the built-in Symbol.iterator; see "Well-Known Symbols" in Chapter 7), then it repeatedly calls the iterator and assigns its produced value to the loop iteration variable.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Standard built-in values in JavaScript that are by default iterables (or provide them) include:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Arrays</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Strings</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Generators (see Chapter 3)</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Collections / TypedArrays (see Chapter 5)</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Warning: Plain objects are not by default suitable for for..of looping. That's because they don't have a default iterator, which is intentional, not a mistake. However, we won't go any further into those nuanced reasonings here. In "Iterators" in Chapter 3, we'll see how to define iterators for our own objects, which lets for..of loop over any object to get a set of values we define.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Here's how to loop over the characters in a primitive string:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (var c of "hello") {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( c );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// "h" "e" "l" "l" "o"</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">The "hello" primitive string value is coerced/boxed to the String object wrapper equivalent, which is an iterable by default.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">In for (XYZ of ABC).., the XYZ clause can either be an assignment expression or a declaration, identical to that same clause in for and for..in loops. So you can do stuff like this:</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">var o = {};</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for (o.a of [1,2,3]) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; &nbsp; console.log( o.a );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for ({x: o.a} of [ {x: 1}, {x: 2}, {x: 3} ]) {</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">&nbsp; console.log( o.a );</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">}</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">// 1 2 3</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">for..of loops can be prematurely stopped, just like other loops, with break, continue, return (if in a function), and thrown exceptions. In any of these cases, the iterator's return(..) function is automatically called (if one exists) to let the iterator perform cleanup tasks, if necessary.</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Note: See "Iterators" in Chapter 3 for more complete coverage on iterables and iterators.</span></font></h2>
### regular expressions
<h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Regular Expressions</span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;"><br></span></font></h2><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 1em; margin-bottom: 16px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 0.3em; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-color: rgb(238, 238, 238);"><font face="Helvetica Neue, Helvetica, Segoe UI, Arial, freesans, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 24.5px; line-height: 30.0125px;">Let's face it: regular expressions haven't changed much in JS in a long time. So it's a great thing that they've finally learned a couple of new tricks in ES6.
